#a gift of onions
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2000
	desc = VIETmisc.2000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
   
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
	}
		option = {
			name = VIETmisc.2000.a
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = {
						trait = incapable
					}
					war = no
					prisoner = no
					age = 16
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
				}
				reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_happy
					who = ROOT
					years = 1
				}
			}
			prestige = 1
		}
}

		is_abroad = no
	}
		weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = gregarious
			}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = shy
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = diligent
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = charitable
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = cruel
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = wroth
				}
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2001.a
				add_character_modifier = {
						name = highly_amused_ruler
						duration = 365
				}
		}
}

# cabbages are too lowly
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2002
		desc = VIETmisc.2002.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
		is_triggered_only = yes
		min_age = 16
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no
		trigger = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				any_courtier = {
							NOT = { trait = incapable }
						war = no
						prisoner = no
						age = 16
						in_command = no
						is_abroad = no
						OR = {
								trait = proud
								trait = gluttonous
								trait = arbitrary
						}
				}
		}
		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gregarious
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = shy
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = ambitious
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = content
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = paranoid
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = trusting
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = just
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = arbitrary
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = kind
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = cruel
				}
		}
		option = { # agree
				name = VIETmisc.2002.a
				random_list = {
						70 = {}
						30 = { add_trait = proud }
				}
				random_courtier = {
						limit = {
								NOT = {
										trait = incapable
								}
								war = no
								prisoner = no
								age = 16
								in_command = no
								is_abroad = no
								OR = {
										trait = proud
										trait = gluttonous
										trait = arbitrary
								}
						}
						opinion = {
								modifier = opinion_satisfied
								who = ROOT
								years = 1
						}
				}
		}
		option = { # disagree
				name = VIETmisc.2002.b
				random_list = {
						70 = {}
						30 = { add_trait = humble }
				}
				random_courtier = {
						limit = {
								NOT = {
										trait = incapable
								}
								war = no
								prisoner = no
								age = 16
								in_command = no
								is_abroad = no
								OR = {
										trait = proud
										trait = gluttonous
										trait = arbitrary
								}
						}
						opinion = {
								modifier = opinion_disappointed
								who = ROOT
								years = 1
						}
				}
		}
}

# onion hair loss treatment
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2003
		desc = VIETmisc.2003.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_recovery
		is_triggered_only = yes
		min_age = 40
		only_men = yes
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no
		trigger = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no		
		}
		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = paranoid
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = trusting
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = stressed
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = content
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = wroth
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = depressed
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = strong
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = envious
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
				}
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2003.a
				prestige = -2
		}
}

# garlic vampires
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2004
		desc = VIETmisc.2004.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
		is_triggered_only = yes
		min_age = 16
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no
		trigger = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no		
				OR = {
						culture_group = central_germanic
						culture_group = west_slavic
						culture_group = south_slavic
						culture_group = baltic
						culture_group = east_slavic
						culture = hungarian
						culture = italian
				}
		}
		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = paranoid
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = trusting
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = stressed
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = content
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = cynical
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = zealous
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = depressed
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = diligent
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
				}
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2004.a
				random_list = {
						80 = {}
						20 = { add_trait = paranoid }
				}				
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2004.b
				if = {
						limit = {
								NOT = { religion_group = pagan_group }
						}
						piety = 4
				}
				prestige = -5
				random_list = {
						70 = {}
						30 = { add_trait = cynical }
				}				
		}
}

# Greek salad
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2006
		desc = VIETmisc.2006.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest_greek
		is_triggered_only = yes
		min_age = 16
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no
		trigger = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no		
				OR = {
						culture_group = byzantine
						capital_scope = {
										culture_group = byzantine
						}
				}
		}
		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gluttonous
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = temperate
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = just
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = arbitrary
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = diligent
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = kind
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = cruel
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = wroth
				}
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2005.a
				if = {
						limit = {
								trait = stressed
						}
						random_list = {
								90 = {}
								10 = { remove_trait = stressed }
						}
				}
				if = {
						limit = {
								trait = depressed
						}
						random_list = {
								90 = {}
								10 = { remove_trait = depressed }
						}
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
						name = eating_good_food
						duration = 180
				}
		}
}

#Chicory
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2010
		desc = VIETmisc.2010.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_illness
		is_triggered_only = yes

		min_age = 16
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no

		trigger = {
			war = no
			in_command = no
			is_abroad = no
			culture_group = central_germanic 
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events
				value = on
			}
		}

		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gregarious
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = shy
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gluttonous
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = temperate
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = weak
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = strong
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = wroth
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = trusting
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = paranoid
				}
		}

		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2010.a
				random_list = {
			90 = {}
			10 = { add_trait = wounded }
		}
		}
}

#Greek bitter greens
character_event = {
		id = VIETmisc.2011
		desc = VIETmisc.2011.desc
		picture = GFX_evt_vegetarian
		is_triggered_only = yes

		min_age = 16
		only_rulers = yes
		capable_only = yes
		prisoner = no

		trigger = {
				war = no
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
		NOT = { 
			culture_group = byzantine
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			culture_group = byzantine
		}		
		}

		weight_multiplier = {
				days = 1
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gregarious
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = shy
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = gluttonous
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = temperate
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = proud
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = wroth
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = patient
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = just
				}
				modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = arbitrary
				}
		}

		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2011.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_tried_something_new
			duration = 365
		}			  
		}
		option = {
				name = VIETmisc.2011.b
		random_list = {
			75 = {}
			25 = { add_trait = proud }

character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2020
	desc = VIETmisc.2020.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no	
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = { # stuffed with vegetables
		name = VIETmisc.2020.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = { add_trait = temperate }
				70 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { remove_trait = gluttonous }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 80
		}
	}

	option = { # stuffed with meat
		name = VIETmisc.2020.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 160
		}
	}


	option = { # stuffed with milk, cream, or cheese
		name = VIETmisc.2020.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { add_trait = gluttonous }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = temperate
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { remove_trait = temperate }
				50 = {}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 320
		}
	}

}

# Meeting Ankou (aka traditional Breton analogue to the grim reaper)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2026
	desc = VIETmisc.2026.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_nightmare

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no
		culture = breton
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = drunkard
		}
	}

	option = {#help him
		name = VIETmisc.2026.a
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
		add_trait = kind
		character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2027 tooltip = VIETmisc.2027.tooltip }
	}
	option = {#run away
		name = VIETmisc.2026.b
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = craven }
			10 = { add_trait = paranoid }			
		}			
	}
	option = {#ignore 
		name = VIETmisc.2026.c
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
	}
}

				}

		}

# The Hourglass
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2045
	desc = VIETmisc.2045.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = yes
		war = no
		in_command = no
		year = 1200
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_has_hourglass }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { year = 1350 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.2045.a"  #ok
		set_character_flag = VIET_has_hourglass
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_efficient_time
			duration = 1111
		}
	}	
}

			60 = {}
		}
	}	
}

# Noontime hijinks
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2049
	desc = VIETmisc.2049.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = yes
		war = no
		in_command = no
		month = 4
		NOT = { month = 9 }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gardener
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = scholar
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.2049.a"  #ok
		random = {
			chance = 5
			add_trait = ill
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = diligent
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				remove_trait = diligent
			}
		}
	}		
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.2049.b"  #ok
		tooltip_info = diligent
		trigger = {
			trait = diligent
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait = ill
		}
	}	
}

# Lost A Ring
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2050
	desc = VIETmisc.2050.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { trait = perceptive }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 3
					trait = absentminded
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gluttonous
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = temperate
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slow
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = quick
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = imbecile
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = genius
			}
	}

	option = {#ok...
		name = VIETmisc.2050.a
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {}
				50 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2056 } } #ring found
			}
		}
		prestige = -2
	}
	option = {#dont worry
		name = VIETmisc.2050.b
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {}
				20 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2056 } } #ring found
			}
		}
		prestige = -4
		piety = 2
	}
}

# Sad Courtier
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2051
	desc = VIETmisc.2051.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_journey_to_spirit_world_altaic #HORSEY

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			prisoner = no
			is_abroad = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				prisoner = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_courtier
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = depressed
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = perceptive
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = absentminded
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = cruel
			}
	}

	option = {#ok...
		name = VIETmisc.2051.a
		event_target:target_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#envy
		name = VIETmisc.2051.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = kind }
		}
		event_target:target_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			30 = { add_trait = envious }
		}
	}
}

	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = content
			}
	}

	option = {#ignore it
		name = VIETmisc.2057.a
		prestige = 1
	}
	option = {#inspect it!
		name = VIETmisc.2057.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { add_trait = greedy }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				trait = charitable
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { remove_trait = charitable }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_beggar_corpse_inspect }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2058 } }
				70 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2059 } }
				5 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2060 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			add_friend = ROOT
			set_character_flag = sunset_watching_buddy
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = VIET_sunset_watcher
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = sunset_watching_buddy
	}
}

				NOT = { trait = ambitious }

			}

				who = ROOT

			}

		}
		piety = 5

			}

			}

			}

			}
		}

# Shaft Head Tilts
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2098
	desc = VIETmisc.2098.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 30
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_shaft_head_tilt }
		NOT = { trait = infirm }
		NOT = { trait = hunchback }
		OR = {
			diplomacy = 11
			intrigue = 11
		}
		diplomacy = 8
		intrigue = 8
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = depressed
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = stressed
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = zealous
			}
	}

	option = {#Yesssss head tilts
		name = VIETmisc.2098.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_shaft_head_tilt
			duration = 2222
		}		
	}
	option = {#No head tilts
		name = VIETmisc.2098.b
		piety = 5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = the_prude
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		religion_group = muslim
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_loves_toothbrushing }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = hedonist
		}
	}

	option = {#Ok
		name = VIETmisc.2101.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_loves_toothbrushing
			duration = -1
		}
		piety = 5
	}
	option = {#Nay
		name = VIETmisc.2101.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { add_trait = cynical }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = zealous
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { remove_trait = zealous }
				50 = {}
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Weird fanservice
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2114
	desc = VIETmisc.2114.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news_female

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = poet
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = impaler
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning = 13
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { learning = 7 }
		}
	}

	option = {#yesyesyes
		name = VIETmisc.2114.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_feeling_sexy
			duration = 365
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				any_lover = {
					opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_sexy_times
							who = ROOT
							years = 3
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				any_lover = {
					opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_disturbing_fetish
							who = ROOT
							years = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#nonono
		name = VIETmisc.2114.b
		piety = 3
	}
}

# Saw someone hot, never see them again
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2119
	desc = VIETmisc.2119.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_market

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
	}

	option = {#imagation!
		name = VIETmisc.2119.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_admiring_eye_candy
			duration = 285
		}		
	}
	option = {#ignore temptation!
		name = VIETmisc.2119.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_resists_temptation
			duration = 456
		}		
	}
}

# Silly infidels

	id = VIETmisc.2122
	desc = VIETmisc.2122.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic_muslim

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			##religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			higher_tier_than = duke
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			lower_tier_than = duke
		}
	}

	option = {#Yessiree

}

# Difficult to approach sibling?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2125
	desc = VIETmisc.2125.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = brave
		}
	}

	option = {#Must worship Ahura Mazda
		name = VIETmisc.2125.a
		piety = 5
	}
	option = {#I'm becoming evil
		name = VIETmisc.2125.b
		piety = -5
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = cynical }
			20 = { add_trait = chaste }
		}
	}
}

# Courtier of a different religion doesn't like sibling love
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2127
	desc = VIETmisc.2127.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = content }
			NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			#NOT = { religion = messalian }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = proud
				trait = wroth
				trait = gregarious
				trait = envious
				trait = cruel
				trait = lustful
				trait = chaste
				trait = temperate
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {#Buzz off
		name = VIETmisc.2127.a
		piety = 5
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = content }
				NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
				#NOT = { religion = messalian }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = proud
					trait = wroth
					trait = gregarious
					trait = envious
					trait = cruel
					trait = lustful
					trait = chaste
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_disgusted
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#Silly
		name = VIETmisc.2127.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_religiously_tolerant_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Visiting foreigner learns the shocking truth
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2133
	desc = VIETmisc.2133.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2133.a
		prestige = 1
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_traveler_learns_about_incest }
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2133.b
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			any_spouse = {
				sibling = ROOT
			}
		}
		prestige = 1
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_traveler_learns_about_incest }
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2133.c
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			any_spouse = {
				sibling = ROOT
			}
		}
		prestige = 1
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_traveler_learns_about_incest }
	}
}

# THERE IS NO HOPE AGAINST TRUTH
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2136
	desc = VIETmisc.2136.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_icon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			prestige = 2000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2136.a
		random_list = {
			50 = { prestige = 2 }
			50 = { piety = 2 }
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2138.a
		piety = 1
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = highly_amused_ruler
			duration = 357
		}
	}
}

#		}
	}

			factor = 2

		}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}

		}
		modifier = {

		}

		}

# New hummus in town
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2141
	desc = VIETmisc.2141.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = south_semitic
			culture_group = east_semitic
			culture_group = northwest_semitic
			culture_group = central_semitic
			culture = hebrew
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2140.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_great_hummus
			duration = 444
		}
	}
}

# Hummus varieties
character_event = {

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

		days = 1

			factor = 2

		}

			factor = 0.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

			name = VIET_great_hummus
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2142.c
		random_list = {
			50 = { piety = 2 }
			50 = { prestige = 2 }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_great_hummus
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2142.d
		prestige = 2
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_great_hummus
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Not enough hummus
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2145
	desc = VIETmisc.2145.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = south_semitic
			culture_group = east_semitic
			culture_group = northwest_semitic
			culture_group = central_semitic
			culture = hebrew
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = charitable
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2145.a
		prestige = -1
	}
}

# Hummus addict
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2147
	desc = VIETmisc.2147.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_hummus_addict }
		OR = {
			culture_group = south_semitic
			culture_group = east_semitic
			culture_group = northwest_semitic
			culture_group = central_semitic
			culture = hebrew
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}	
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2147.a
		health = 0.3
		set_character_flag = VIET_hummus_addict
	}
}

# Fine hummus region rising
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2152
	desc = VIETmisc.2152.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			culture_group = south_semitic
			culture_group = east_semitic
			culture_group = northwest_semitic
			culture_group = central_semitic
			culture = hebrew
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region }
		NOT = { has_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter }
		NOT = {
			kingdom = {
				ROOT = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							ROOT = {
								kingdom = {
									PREVPREV = {
										any_realm_province = {
											kingdom = {
												title = PREVPREVPREV
											}
											has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}	
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3456
	}

	option = {#not ok
		name = VIETmisc.2152.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_hummus_producing_region
			duration = -1
		}
		set_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter
	}
}

# Fine hummus region declining
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2153
	desc = VIETmisc.2153.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
		had_province_flag = { flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter days = 7300 } 
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}	
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1234
	}

	option = {#not ok
		name = VIETmisc.2153.a
		remove_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
		clr_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter
	}
}



# The great hummus debate
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2154
	desc = VIETmisc.2154.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = south_semitic
			culture_group = east_semitic
			culture_group = northwest_semitic
			culture_group = central_semitic

# Hummus gift from locals
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2159
	desc = VIETmisc.2159.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_given_hummus_gift }
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 800
	}

	option = {#not ok
		name = VIETmisc.2159.a
		owner = {
			set_character_flag = VIET_given_hummus_gift
			prestige = 10
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_great_hummus
				duration = 365
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

# Sibling sexy times 3
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2170
	desc = VIETmisc.2170.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_lovers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
#		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			#religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
#		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
			opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
		}
		NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2170.a
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
		piety = 5
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
			}
			piety = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 }
					NOT = { is_lover = ROOT }
				}
				random = {
					add_lover = ROOT
					chance = 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2170.b
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
		piety = 5
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
			}
			piety = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 }
					NOT = { is_lover = ROOT }
				}
				random = {
					add_lover = ROOT
					chance = 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2172
	desc = VIETmisc.2172.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_marriage_zoroastrian_group

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		religion_group = zoroastrian_group
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			religion = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2172.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				religion = ROOT			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = agrees_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2172.b
		random_list = {
			75 = { }
			25 = { add_trait = zealous }
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				religion = ROOT			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = disagrees_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

			trait = diligent
		}

			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning = 14
		}

			factor = 0.5

		}

		NOT = {
			any_courtier = {
				has_character_modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_incest
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
			NOT = { trait = imbecile }
			NOT = { trait = slow }
			religion = ROOT
			diplomacy = 8
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = scholar
				trait = quick
				trait = genius
				trait = charismatic_negotiator
				trait = grey_eminence
				learning = 14
				AND = {
					trait = lustful
					diplomacy = 11
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_incest }
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning = 12
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { learning = 8 }
		}
	}

	option = {#creepy
		name = VIETmisc.2188.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = imbecile }
				NOT = { trait = slow }
				religion = ROOT
				diplomacy = 8
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = scholar
					trait = quick
					trait = genius
					trait = charismatic_negotiator
					trait = grey_eminence
					learning = 14
					AND = {
						trait = lustful
						diplomacy = 11
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_obsessed_with_incest
				duration = 5555
			}

				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 30
		}
	}

		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = humble }
			}
			random = {

				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}

		}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2199.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2199.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = the_prude
			duration = 365
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = temperate
			chance = 10
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2199.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = celibate }
			NOT = { trait = chaste }
			NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_feeling_sexy 
			duration = 582
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = lustful
			chance = 20
		}
	}
}

# watching ye, scum
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2205
	desc = VIETmisc.2205.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = VIET_blatant_TES }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = greedy 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_patrician = yes
				is_merchant_republic = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			tier = emperor
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2205.a
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 15
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2205.b
		piety = 3
	}
}

# Guard duty
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2209
	desc = VIETmisc.2209.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_large_army

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		#war = no
		OR = {
			OR = {
				any_war = {
					holy_war_trigger = yes
				}
				any_liege = {
					any_war = {
						holy_war_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				any_war = {
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = WAGING_CRUSADE
						hidden_tooltip = {
							crusade_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
				any_liege = {
					any_war = {
						custom_tooltip = {
							text = WAGING_CRUSADE
							hidden_tooltip = {
								crusade_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#in_command = no
		#is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = VIET_blatant_TES }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2209.a
		prestige = 2
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2209.b
		piety = 2
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2209.c
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 20
		}
	}
}

# Maybe I'm le dragonborn
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2210
	desc = VIETmisc.2210.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_holy_light_zoroastrian_group

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		religion_group = zoroastrian_group
		NOT = { has_global_flag = VIET_blatant_TES }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = saoshyant_appears }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = deceitful 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2210.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = highly_amused_ruler
			duration = 441
		}		
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2210.b
		piety = 2	
	}
}

# Nazeem
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2213
	desc = VIETmisc.2213.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_market

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			trait = proud
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = VIET_blatant_TES }
		NOT = { tier = baron }
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2213.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				trait = proud
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}			
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_annoyed_ruler
			duration = 456
		}
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 10
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2213.b
		piety = 3
		random = {
			add_trait = patient
			chance = 5
		}
	}
}

# visiting a farmer
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2220
	desc = VIETmisc.2220.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2220.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 444
		}
	}
	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2220.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = advice_giver
			duration = 444
		}
	}
}

	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

			factor = 0.5

			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}

		}

# Kill a child
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2226
	desc = VIETmisc.2226.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_vikings_arriving_oldgods

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_men = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_dlc = "The Old Gods"
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_raid_child_kill }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2226.a
		random = {
			add_trait = just
			chance = 5
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_raid_child_kill
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2226.b
		random = {
			add_trait = cruel
			chance = 80
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			remove_trait = kind
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_raid_child_kill
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2226.c
		random = {
			add_trait = depressed
			chance = 10
		}
		piety = 5
		set_character_flag = VIET_raid_child_kill
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2226.d
		random_list = {
			30 = { add_trait = kind }
			15 = { add_trait = trusting }
			5 = { add_trait = just }
			50 = { }
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_raid_child_kill
	}
}

# Present for wife?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2239
	desc = VIETmisc.2239.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_vikings_arriving_oldgods

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_men = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_dlc = "The Old Gods"
		is_married = yes
		spouse = {
			NOT = { age = 50 }
			NOT = { trait = ugly }
			NOT = { trait = hunchback }
			NOT = { trait = wrymouth }
			ai = yes
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2239.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_feeling_sexy
			duration = 480
		}
		spouse = {
			opinion = {
					modifier = VIET_opinion_great_gift
					who = ROOT
					years = 2
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_feeling_sexy
				duration = 480
			}
		}

		}
	}

# child wets bed
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2245
	desc = VIETmisc.2245.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_nightmare

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 2
	max_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
	}

	option = {#...
		name = VIETmisc.2245.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { age = 8 }
		}
		prestige = -1
	}
	option = {#...
		name = VIETmisc.2245.b
		trigger = {
			age = 8
		}
		prestige = -5
	}
	option = {#...
		name = VIETmisc.2245.c
		trigger = {
			age = 13
			is_female = no
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = lustful
			chance = 10
		}
		prestige = -5
	}
	option = {#...
		name = VIETmisc.2245.d
		trigger = {
			age = 13
			is_female = no
			OR = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				#religion = messalian
			}
			any_sibling = {
				is_female = yes
			}
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = lustful
			chance = 10
		}
		prestige = -5
	}
}

	id = VIETmisc.2246
	desc = VIETmisc.2246.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = absentminded  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = perceptive
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
	}

	option = {#...
		name = VIETmisc.2246.a
		prestige = -1
	}
}

	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

		is_abroad = no

			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { health = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			health = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = weak
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = strong
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2249.a
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_gotta_go_1 }
		prestige = -5
	}
	option = {#no
		name = VIETmisc.2249.b
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_gotta_go_2 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				40 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2250 } }
				60 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2251 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plans criticized
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2256
	desc = VIETmisc.2256.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = yes
		#in_command = no
		#is_abroad = no
		martial = 8
		any_courtier = {
			age = 10
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				martial = 10
				trait = genius
				trait = quick
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent   
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2256.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					martial = 10
					trait = genius
					trait = quick
				}			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = agrees_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = listens_to_others
			duration = 482
		}
	}
	option = {#no
		name = VIETmisc.2256.b
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					martial = 10
					trait = genius
					trait = quick
				}			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = disagrees_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			prestige = -5
		}
		prestige = 5
	}
	option = {#well...
		name = VIETmisc.2256.c
		tooltip_info = genius
		trigger = {
			trait = genius
			NOT = { trait = quick }
			NOT = { martial = 11 }
		}		
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					martial = 10
					trait = genius
					trait = quick
				}			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_impressed
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
	}
	option = {#well...
		name = VIETmisc.2256.c
		tooltip_info = quick
		trigger = {
			trait = quick 
			NOT = { trait = genius }
			NOT = { martial = 11 }
		}		
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					martial = 10
					trait = genius
					trait = quick
				}			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_impressed
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
	}
	option = {#well...
		name = VIETmisc.2256.c
		tooltip_info = martial
		trigger = {
			martial = 11
			NOT = { trait = quick }
			NOT = { trait = genius }
		}		
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 10
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					martial = 10
					trait = genius
					trait = quick
				}			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_impressed
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
		}
		prestige = 10
	}
}

	only_rulers = yes

	prisoner = no

		war = yes
		#in_command = no
		#is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent   
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			martial = 12
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { martial = 7 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2257.a
		prestige = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2257.b
		piety = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

# Useful ideas for war effort
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2258
	desc = VIETmisc.2258.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = yes
		#in_command = no
		#is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_war_ideas }
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					OR = {
						martial = 10
						trait = skilled_tactician
						trait = brilliant_strategist
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					OR = {
						martial = 18
						AND = {
							trait = skilled_tactician
							martial = 13
						}
						AND = {
							trait = brilliant_strategist
							martial = 13
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent   
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2258.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_war_ideas
			duration = 730
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_female = no
						OR = {
							martial = 10
							trait = skilled_tactician
							trait = brilliant_strategist
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_female = yes
						OR = {
							martial = 18
							AND = {
								trait = skilled_tactician
								martial = 13
							}
							AND = {
								trait = brilliant_strategist
								martial = 13
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = respected_opinion
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_helped_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

# shiny pebbles
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2274
	desc = VIETmisc.2274.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2274.a
		piety = 2
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2274.b
		trigger = {
			any_child = {
				NOT = { is_adult = yes }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
		}
		any_child = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_adult = yes }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_great_gift
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Sulfur treatment
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2278
	desc = VIETmisc.2278.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = stressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = fair
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2278.a
		wealth = -3
		random = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_bad_acne
				duration = 450
			}
			chance = 15
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2278.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_skeptical_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		random = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_bad_acne
				duration = 450
			}
			chance = 30
		}
	}
}

# Paneer
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2279
	desc = VIETmisc.2279.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2279.a
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_paneeer_1 }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 224
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2279.b
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_paneeer_2 }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 224
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2279.c
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_paneeer_3 }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 224
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2279.d
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_paneeer_4 }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 224
		}
	}
}

# Parathra Bread
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2281
	desc = VIETmisc.2281.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = deceitful
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2281.a
		prestige = 1
		piety = 1
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2281.b
		piety = 2
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2281.c
		random_list = {
			50 = { prestige = 2 }
			50 = { piety = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2281.d
		prestige = 2
	}
}

# Kebab spreads!
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2284
	desc = VIETmisc.2284.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
		}
		year = 900
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				empire = { title = e_india }
				#empire = { title = e_south_india } #this title doesn't exist in the mod
				empire = { title = e_tamil }
				empire = { title = e_deccan }
				empire = { title = e_rajastan }
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2284.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_loves_kebabs
			duration = 911
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2284.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_hates_kebabs
			duration = 911
		}
	}
}
