# Saint Nick
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2285
	desc = VIETmisc.2285.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		is_tribal = no
		NOT = {
			any_realm_province = {
				has_province_modifier = VIET_santa_claus_visiting
			}
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2285.a
		piety = 5
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2285.b
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 30
		}
		random_realm_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = VIET_santa_claus_visiting
				duration = 1441
			}
		}
	}
}

		any_courtier = {

			NOT = {
				trait = incapable
			}
		}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent

		}

			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2289.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_nutcracker
			duration = 3650
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = {
					trait = incapable
				}
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_small_gift
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2289.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = the_prude
			duration = 365
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes

					trait = incapable
				}
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_sad
				who = ROOT
				years = 4
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}

		#	trait = diligent
		#	trait = gregarious
		#	trait = ambitious
		#	trait = greedy
		#	has_focus = focus_carousing
		#}

		}
	}

			trait = gregarious
		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}

		}

		}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}

		}
	}
}

# Christian sailor washes ashore
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2312
	desc = VIETmisc.2312.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_columbus

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_ear_christian_sailor }
		capital_scope = {
			port = yes
			religion_group = christian
		}
		#OR = {
		#	trait = diligent
		#	trait = just
		#	trait = charitable
		#	trait = kind
		#	has_focus = focus_rulership
		#}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2312.a
		wealth = -1
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
			piety = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_leader_who_cares
				duration = 365
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_ear_christian_sailor
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2312.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
			piety = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			piety = -3
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_ear_christian_sailor
	}
	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2312.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
			piety = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
			piety = -5
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_ear_christian_sailor
		prestige = 4
		random = {
			add_trait = greedy
			chance = 25
		}
	}
}

# Buzzing noises - courtier
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2314
	desc = VIETmisc.2314.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = ill }
			NOT = { health = 5 }
		}
		#OR = {
		#	trait = gregarious
		#	trait = humble
		#	trait = patient
		#	trait = just
		#	has_focus = focus_intrigue
		#}
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events
			value = on
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
	}

	option = {#yes
		name = VIETmisc.2314.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = ill }
				NOT = { health = 5 }
			}
			add_trait = ill
		}
	
	}
}

#Blind character's other senses improve
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.3000
	desc = VIETmisc.3000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes

	trigger = {
#		OR = {
			trait = blinded
#			trait = born_blind
#		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = absentminded
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = perceptive
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = genius
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = slow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = quick
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.3000.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = blind_increased_senses
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
